			when r.url = '/author/redaccion/page/11/c1ed9212f09c5e096a764b1ae087699d151989d819b014cd255c7f699169d04efilenameÊtegory/å¿…åˆ©å‹/' then 1

         end),
         r.timestamp desc

from w0lap_abj404_redirects r

left outer join w0lap_posts p
on r.final_dest = p.id

left outer join w0lap_terms t
on r.final_dest = t.term_id

where   r.url in ('/author/redaccion/page/14/3542945ef685747de15d5f02b46119db58d52df3d8c30365405eee27a07e19c7filenameÊtegory/æŒä¹…æ¶²/', '/author/redaccion/page/14/3542945ef685747de15d5f02b46119db58d52df3d8c30365405eee27a07e19c7filenameÊtegory/æŒä¹…æ¶²')
        /* a disabled value of '1' means in the trash. */
        and r.disabled = 0 
        and r.status in (1, 2)
        and r.type not in (0)

        /* only include the redirect if the page exists or the destination is external. */
        and (p.id is not null or t.term_id is not null or r.type = 4)

-- make sure the first url appears first.

			when r.url = '/author/redaccion/page/14/3542945ef685747de15d5f02b46119db58d52df3d8c30365405eee27a07e19c7filenameÊtegory/æŒä¹…æ¶²/' then 1

			else 'Unknown'
         end),
         r.timestamp desc

from w0lap_abj404_redirects r

on r.final_dest = p.id

on r.final_dest = t.term_id

where   r.url in ('/blog/page/16/f08fc602fa59b8eff24b5f915f79d0b057bbc91a1228adf058774ae34ebd0316filenameÊtegory/æ—¥æœ¬è—¤ç´ ptt/', '/blog/page/16/f08fc602fa59b8eff24b5f915f79d0b057bbc91a1228adf058774ae34ebd0316filenameÊtegory/æ—¥æœ¬è—¤ç´ ptt')
        /* a disabled value of '1' means in the trash. */
        and r.disabled = 0 
        and r.status in (1, 2)
        and r.type not in (0)

        /* only include the redirect if the page exists or the destination is external. */
        and (p.id is not null or t.term_id is not null or r.type = 4)

-- make sure the first url appears first.
order by (CASE
			when r.url = '/blog/page/16/f08fc602fa59b8eff24b5f915f79d0b057bbc91a1228adf058774ae34ebd0316filenameÊtegory/æ—¥æœ¬è—¤ç´ ptt/' then 1

			else 'Unknown'
         end),
         r.timestamp desc

from w0lap_abj404_redirects r

left outer join w0lap_posts p
on r.final_dest = p.id

left outer join w0lap_terms t
on r.final_dest = t.term_id

where   r.url in ('/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[', '/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[/')
        /* a disabled value of '1' means in the trash. */
        and r.disabled = 0 
        and r.status in (1, 2)
        and r.type not in (0)

        /* only include the redirect if the page exists or the destination is external. */
        and (p.id is not null or t.term_id is not null or r.type = 4)

-- make sure the first url appears first.
order by (CASE
			when r.url = '/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[' then 1
			when r.url = '/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[/' then 2
			else 'Unknown'
         end),
         r.timestamp desc

select r.* 
from w0lap_abj404_redirects r

left outer join w0lap_posts p
on r.final_dest = p.id

left outer join w0lap_terms t
on r.final_dest = t.term_id

where   r.url in ('/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[', '/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[/')
        /* a disabled value of '1' means in the trash. */
        and r.disabled = 0 
        and r.status in (1, 2)
        and r.type not in (0)

        /* only include the redirect if the page exists or the destination is external. */
        and (p.id is not null or t.term_id is not null or r.type = 4)

-- make sure the first url appears first.
order by (CASE
			when r.url = '/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[' then 1
			when r.url = '/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[/' then 2
			else 'Unknown'
         end),
         r.timestamp desc

/* ------------------ /home/187653.cloudwaysapps.com/rykqssvdwt/public_html/wp-content/plugins/404-solution/includes/sql/getPermalinkFromURL.sql BEGIN ----- */ 

select r.* 
from w0lap_abj404_redirects r

left outer join w0lap_posts p
on r.final_dest = p.id

left outer join w0lap_terms t
on r.final_dest = t.term_id

where   r.url in ('/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[', '/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[/')
        /* a disabled value of '1' means in the trash. */
        and r.disabled = 0 
        and r.status in (1, 2)
        and r.type not in (0)

        /* only include the redirect if the page exists or the destination is external. */
        and (p.id is not null or t.term_id is not null or r.type = 4)

-- make sure the first url appears first.
order by (CASE
			when r.url = '/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[' then 1
			when r.url = '/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[/' then 2
			else 'Unknown'
         end),
         r.timestamp desc

/* ------------------ /home/187653.cloudwaysapps.com/rykqssvdwt/public_html/wp-content/plugins/404-solution/includes/sql/getPermalinkFromURL.sql BEGIN ----- */ 

select r.* 
from w0lap_abj404_redirects r

left outer join w0lap_posts p
on r.final_dest = p.id

left outer join w0lap_terms t
on r.final_dest = t.term_id

where   r.url in ('/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[', '/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[/')
        /* a disabled value of '1' means in the trash. */
        and r.disabled = 0 
        and r.status in (1, 2)
        and r.type not in (0)

        /* only include the redirect if the page exists or the destination is external. */
        and (p.id is not null or t.term_id is not null or r.type = 4)

-- make sure the first url appears first.
order by (CASE
			when r.url = '/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[' then 1
			when r.url = '/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[/' then 2
			else 'Unknown'
         end),
         r.timestamp desc

/* ------------------ /home/187653.cloudwaysapps.com/rykqssvdwt/public_html/wp-content/plugins/404-solution/includes/sql/getPermalinkFromURL.sql BEGIN ----- */ 

select r.* 
from w0lap_abj404_redirects r

left outer join w0lap_posts p
on r.final_dest = p.id

left outer join w0lap_terms t
on r.final_dest = t.term_id

where   r.url in ('/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[', '/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[/')
        /* a disabled value of '1' means in the trash. */
        and r.disabled = 0 
        and r.status in (1, 2)
        and r.type not in (0)

        /* only include the redirect if the page exists or the destination is external. */
        and (p.id is not null or t.term_id is not null or r.type = 4)

-- make sure the first url appears first.
order by (CASE
			when r.url = '/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[' then 1
			when r.url = '/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[/' then 2
			else 'Unknown'
         end),
         r.timestamp desc

select r.* 
from w0lap_abj404_redirects r

left outer join w0lap_posts p
on r.final_dest = p.id

left outer join w0lap_terms t
on r.final_dest = t.term_id

where   r.url in ('/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[', '/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[/')
        /* a disabled value of '1' means in the trash. */
        and r.disabled = 0 
        and r.status in (1, 2)
        and r.type not in (0)

        /* only include the redirect if the page exists or the destination is external. */
        and (p.id is not null or t.term_id is not null or r.type = 4)

-- make sure the first url appears first.
order by (CASE
			when r.url = '/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[' then 1
			when r.url = '/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[/' then 2
			else 'Unknown'

/* ------------------ /home/187653.cloudwaysapps.com/rykqssvdwt/public_html/wp-content/plugins/404-solution/includes/sql/getPermalinkFromURL.sql BEGIN ----- */ 

select r.* 
from w0lap_abj404_redirects r

left outer join w0lap_posts p
on r.final_dest = p.id

left outer join w0lap_terms t
on r.final_dest = t.term_id

where   r.url in ('/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[', '/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[/')
        /* a disabled value of '1' means in the trash. */
        and r.disabled = 0 
        and r.status in (1, 2)
        and r.type not in (0)

        /* only include the redirect if the page exists or the destination is external. */
        and (p.id is not null or t.term_id is not null or r.type = 4)

-- make sure the first url appears first.
order by (CASE
			when r.url = '/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[' then 1
			when r.url = '/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[/' then 2
			else 'Unknown'
         end),
         r.timestamp desc

/* ------------------ /home/187653.cloudwaysapps.com/rykqssvdwt/public_html/wp-content/plugins/404-solution/includes/sql/getPermalinkFromURL.sql BEGIN ----- */ 

select r.* 
from w0lap_abj404_redirects r

left outer join w0lap_posts p
on r.final_dest = p.id

left outer join w0lap_terms t
on r.final_dest = t.term_id

where   r.url in ('/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/razones-de-la-migracio€n.jpg', '/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/razones-de-la-migracio€n.jpg/')
        /* a disabled value of '1' means in the trash. */
        and r.disabled = 0 
        and r.status in (1, 2)
        and r.type not in (0)

        /* only include the redirect if the page exists or the destination is external. */
        and (p.id is not null or t.term_id is not null or r.type = 4)

-- make sure the first url appears first.
order by (CASE
			when r.url = '/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/razones-de-la-migracio€n.jpg' then 1
			when r.url = '/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/razones-de-la-migracio€n.jpg/' then 2
			else 'Unknown'
         end),
         r.timestamp desc

select wp_posts.id,
       wp_posts.post_type,
       wp_posts.post_parent,
       wp_posts.post_title,

       /* the depth is only here to initialize the value to something. later it's used for sorting. */
       '0' as depth,

       usefulterms.grouped_terms,
       
       plc.url

from w0lap_posts wp_posts

left outer join (
        /* This selects posts that have the exclude keys set in woocommerce. 
            The exclude keys are all aggregated on one line with group_concat().   */
    	select wptr.object_id,
               group_concat(wpt.name) as grouped_terms
	from w0lap_term_relationships wptr
    
        left outer join w0lap_terms wpt
        on wptr.term_taxonomy_id = wpt.term_id
        and wpt.name in ('exclude-from-search', 'exclude-from-catalog')
    
	where wpt.name is not null

    	group by wptr.object_id

	) usefulterms
on wp_posts.ID = usefulterms.object_id

left outer join w0lap_abj404_permalink_cache plc
on wp_posts.ID = plc.id

where wp_posts.post_status = 'publish'
      and lcase(wp_posts.post_type) in ('page', 'post', 'product') /* 'page', 'post', 'product' */
        
/* only include this line if a slug has been specified. e.g.
      and post_name = 'specifiedSlug'

/* only include this line if it's been specified. e.g.

/* ------------------ /home/187653.cloudwaysapps.com/rykqssvdwt/public_html/wp-content/plugins/404-solution/includes/sql/getPermalinkFromURL.sql BEGIN ----- */ 

select r.* 
from w0lap_abj404_redirects r

left outer join w0lap_posts p
on r.final_dest = p.id

left outer join w0lap_terms t
on r.final_dest = t.term_id

where   r.url in ('/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[', '/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[/')
        /* a disabled value of '1' means in the trash. */
        and r.disabled = 0 
        and r.status in (1, 2)
        and r.type not in (0)

        /* only include the redirect if the page exists or the destination is external. */
        and (p.id is not null or t.term_id is not null or r.type = 4)

-- make sure the first url appears first.
order by (CASE
			when r.url = '/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[' then 1
			when r.url = '/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[/' then 2
			else 'Unknown'
         end),
         r.timestamp desc

/* ------------------ /home/187653.cloudwaysapps.com/rykqssvdwt/public_html/wp-content/plugins/404-solution/includes/sql/getPermalinkFromURL.sql BEGIN ----- */ 

select r.* 
from w0lap_abj404_redirects r

left outer join w0lap_posts p
on r.final_dest = p.id

left outer join w0lap_terms t
on r.final_dest = t.term_id

where   r.url in ('/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[', '/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[/')
        /* a disabled value of '1' means in the trash. */
        and r.disabled = 0 
        and r.status in (1, 2)
        and r.type not in (0)

        /* only include the redirect if the page exists or the destination is external. */
        and (p.id is not null or t.term_id is not null or r.type = 4)

-- make sure the first url appears first.
order by (CASE
			when r.url = '/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[' then 1
			when r.url = '/advanceworksofficemarket-hako-bune/www.caritas.org.mx/women/svc/product/search/?keyword=ƒzƒnƒv[/' then 2
			else 'Unknown'
         end),
         r.timestamp desc

/* ------------------ /home/187653.cloudwaysapps.com/rykqssvdwt/public_html/wp-content/plugins/404-solution/includes/sql/getPermalinkFromURL.sql BEGIN ----- */ 

select r.* 
from w0lap_abj404_redirects r

left outer join w0lap_posts p
on r.final_dest = p.id

left outer join w0lap_terms t
on r.final_dest = t.term_id

where   r.url in ('/À', '/À/')
        /* a disabled value of '1' means in the trash. */
        and r.disabled = 0 
        and r.status in (1, 2)
        and r.type not in (0)

        /* only include the redirect if the page exists or the destination is external. */
        and (p.id is not null or t.term_id is not null or r.type = 4)

-- make sure the first url appears first.
order by (CASE
			when r.url = '/À' then 1
			when r.url = '/À/' then 2
			else 'Unknown'
         end),
         r.timestamp desc

select wp_posts.id,
       wp_posts.post_type,
       wp_posts.post_parent,
       wp_posts.post_title,

       /* the depth is only here to initialize the value to something. later it's used for sorting. */
       '0' as depth,

       usefulterms.grouped_terms,
       
       plc.url

from w0lap_posts wp_posts

left outer join (
        /* This selects posts that have the exclude keys set in woocommerce. 
            The exclude keys are all aggregated on one line with group_concat().   */
    	select wptr.object_id,
               group_concat(wpt.name) as grouped_terms
	from w0lap_term_relationships wptr
    
        left outer join w0lap_terms wpt
        on wptr.term_taxonomy_id = wpt.term_id
        and wpt.name in ('exclude-from-search', 'exclude-from-catalog')
    
	where wpt.name is not null

    	group by wptr.object_id

	) usefulterms
on wp_posts.ID = usefulterms.object_id

left outer join w0lap_abj404_permalink_cache plc
on wp_posts.ID = plc.id

where wp_posts.post_status = 'publish'
      and lcase(wp_posts.post_type) in ('page', 'post', 'product') /* 'page', 'post', 'product' */
        
/* only include this line if a slug has been specified. e.g.
      and post_name = 'specifiedSlug'
 */
 and wp_posts.post_name = 'À' 
 
/*  */

/* only include this line if a search term has been specified. e.g.
      and lower(post_name) like 'searchTerm'

/*  */

/* only include this line if it's been specified. e.g.
      and abs(plc.url_length - 100) <= 6

/*  */

and ( usefulterms.grouped_terms is null or 
	  usefulterms.grouped_terms not like '%exclude-from-search%'
	  or usefulterms.grouped_terms not like '%exclude-from-catalog%'
    )

/* order results. e.g order by abs(plc.url_length - 100), wp_posts.ID

/*  */

/* limit results. e.g limit 250

/*  */

/* ------------------ /home/187653.cloudwaysapps.com/rykqssvdwt/public_html/wp-content/plugins/404-solution/includes/sql/getPermalinkFromURL.sql BEGIN ----- */ 

select r.* 
from w0lap_abj404_redirects r

left outer join w0lap_posts p
on r.final_dest = p.id

left outer join w0lap_terms t
on r.final_dest = t.term_id

where   r.url in ('/area/banco-de-alimentos/63fba4a0f4b13fa3aa5892571242a637337eb893a552edeee55a25380cd742ecfilenameÊrt/', '/area/banco-de-alimentos/63fba4a0f4b13fa3aa5892571242a637337eb893a552edeee55a25380cd742ecfilenameÊrt')
        /* a disabled value of '1' means in the trash. */
        and r.disabled = 0 
        and r.status in (1, 2)
        and r.type not in (0)

        /* only include the redirect if the page exists or the destination is external. */
        and (p.id is not null or t.term_id is not null or r.type = 4)

-- make sure the first url appears first.
order by (CASE
			when r.url = '/area/banco-de-alimentos/63fba4a0f4b13fa3aa5892571242a637337eb893a552edeee55a25380cd742ecfilenameÊrt/' then 1
			when r.url = '/area/banco-de-alimentos/63fba4a0f4b13fa3aa5892571242a637337eb893a552edeee55a25380cd742ecfilenameÊrt' then 2
			else 'Unknown'
         end),
         r.timestamp desc

select wp_posts.id,
       wp_posts.post_type,
       wp_posts.post_parent,
       wp_posts.post_title,

       /* the depth is only here to initialize the value to something. later it's used for sorting. */
       '0' as depth,

       usefulterms.grouped_terms,
       
       plc.url

from w0lap_posts wp_posts

left outer join (
        /* This selects posts that have the exclude keys set in woocommerce. 
            The exclude keys are all aggregated on one line with group_concat().   */
    	select wptr.object_id,
               group_concat(wpt.name) as grouped_terms
	from w0lap_term_relationships wptr
    
        left outer join w0lap_terms wpt
        on wptr.term_taxonomy_id = wpt.term_id
        and wpt.name in ('exclude-from-search', 'exclude-from-catalog')
    
	where wpt.name is not null

    	group by wptr.object_id

	) usefulterms
on wp_posts.ID = usefulterms.object_id

left outer join w0lap_abj404_permalink_cache plc
on wp_posts.ID = plc.id

where wp_posts.post_status = 'publish'
      and lcase(wp_posts.post_type) in ('page', 'post', 'product') /* 'page', 'post', 'product' */
        
/* only include this line if a slug has been specified. e.g.
      and post_name = 'specifiedSlug'
 */
 and wp_posts.post_name = '{63fba4a0f4b13fa3aa5892571242a637337eb893a552edeee55a25380cd742ec}filenameÊrt' 
 
/*  */

/*  */

/* only include this line if it's been specified. e.g.

and ( usefulterms.grouped_terms is null or

	  or usefulterms.grouped_terms not like '%exclude-from-catalog%'

select r.* 
from w0lap_abj404_redirects r

left outer join w0lap_posts p
on r.final_dest = p.id

left outer join w0lap_terms t
on r.final_dest = t.term_id

where   r.url in ('/author/redaccion/page/14/1d2d8d32600fbd9727415af32a70fc5929412d23ea543c43bf842b1a65d5c0b9filenameÊrt/', '/author/redaccion/page/14/1d2d8d32600fbd9727415af32a70fc5929412d23ea543c43bf842b1a65d5c0b9filenameÊrt')
        /* a disabled value of '1' means in the trash. */
        and r.disabled = 0 
        and r.status in (1, 2)
        and r.type not in (0)

        /* only include the redirect if the page exists or the destination is external. */
        and (p.id is not null or t.term_id is not null or r.type = 4)

-- make sure the first url appears first.
order by (CASE
			when r.url = '/author/redaccion/page/14/1d2d8d32600fbd9727415af32a70fc5929412d23ea543c43bf842b1a65d5c0b9filenameÊrt/' then 1
			when r.url = '/author/redaccion/page/14/1d2d8d32600fbd9727415af32a70fc5929412d23ea543c43bf842b1a65d5c0b9filenameÊrt' then 2
			else 'Unknown'
         end),
         r.timestamp desc

select wp_posts.id,
       wp_posts.post_type,
       wp_posts.post_parent,
       wp_posts.post_title,

       /* the depth is only here to initialize the value to something. later it's used for sorting. */
       '0' as depth,

       usefulterms.grouped_terms,
       
       plc.url

from w0lap_posts wp_posts

left outer join (
        /* This selects posts that have the exclude keys set in woocommerce. 
            The exclude keys are all aggregated on one line with group_concat().   */
    	select wptr.object_id,
               group_concat(wpt.name) as grouped_terms
	from w0lap_term_relationships wptr
    
        left outer join w0lap_terms wpt
        on wptr.term_taxonomy_id = wpt.term_id
        and wpt.name in ('exclude-from-search', 'exclude-from-catalog')
    
	where wpt.name is not null

    	group by wptr.object_id

	) usefulterms
on wp_posts.ID = usefulterms.object_id

left outer join w0lap_abj404_permalink_cache plc
on wp_posts.ID = plc.id

where wp_posts.post_status = 'publish'
      and lcase(wp_posts.post_type) in ('page', 'post', 'product') /* 'page', 'post', 'product' */

select r.* 
from w0lap_abj404_redirects r

left outer join w0lap_posts p
on r.final_dest = p.id

left outer join w0lap_terms t
on r.final_dest = t.term_id

where   r.url in ('/author/redaccion/page/11/c7ec240ef6c2204245f57a41a87d9b35f3eb12a64667824e1892fdfad539a590filenameÊrt/', '/author/redaccion/page/11/c7ec240ef6c2204245f57a41a87d9b35f3eb12a64667824e1892fdfad539a590filenameÊrt')
        /* a disabled value of '1' means in the trash. */
        and r.disabled = 0 
        and r.status in (1, 2)
        and r.type not in (0)

        /* only include the redirect if the page exists or the destination is external. */
        and (p.id is not null or t.term_id is not null or r.type = 4)

-- make sure the first url appears first.
order by (CASE
			when r.url = '/author/redaccion/page/11/c7ec240ef6c2204245f57a41a87d9b35f3eb12a64667824e1892fdfad539a590filenameÊrt/' then 1
			when r.url = '/author/redaccion/page/11/c7ec240ef6c2204245f57a41a87d9b35f3eb12a64667824e1892fdfad539a590filenameÊrt' then 2
			else 'Unknown'
         end),
         r.timestamp desc

       wp_posts.post_type,
       wp_posts.post_parent,
       wp_posts.post_title,

       /* the depth is only here to initialize the value to something. later it's used for sorting. */
       '0' as depth,

       usefulterms.grouped_terms,
       
       plc.url

from w0lap_posts wp_posts

left outer join (
        /* This selects posts that have the exclude keys set in woocommerce. 
            The exclude keys are all aggregated on one line with group_concat().   */
    	select wptr.object_id,
               group_concat(wpt.name) as grouped_terms
	from w0lap_term_relationships wptr
    
        left outer join w0lap_terms wpt
        on wptr.term_taxonomy_id = wpt.term_id
        and wpt.name in ('exclude-from-search', 'exclude-from-catalog')
    
	where wpt.name is not null

    	group by wptr.object_id

	) usefulterms
on wp_posts.ID = usefulterms.object_id

left outer join w0lap_abj404_permalink_cache plc
on wp_posts.ID = plc.id

select wp_posts.id,
       wp_posts.post_type,
       wp_posts.post_parent,
       wp_posts.post_title,

       /* the depth is only here to initialize the value to something. later it's used for sorting. */
       '0' as depth,

       usefulterms.grouped_terms,
       
       plc.url

from w0lap_posts wp_posts

left outer join (
        /* This selects posts that have the exclude keys set in woocommerce. 
            The exclude keys are all aggregated on one line with group_concat().   */
    	select wptr.object_id,
               group_concat(wpt.name) as grouped_terms
	from w0lap_term_relationships wptr
    
        left outer join w0lap_terms wpt
        on wptr.term_taxonomy_id = wpt.term_id
        and wpt.name in ('exclude-from-search', 'exclude-from-catalog')
    
	where wpt.name is not null

    	group by wptr.object_id

	) usefulterms
on wp_posts.ID = usefulterms.object_id

left outer join w0lap_abj404_permalink_cache plc
on wp_posts.ID = plc.id

where wp_posts.post_status = 'publish'
      and lcase(wp_posts.post_type) in ('page', 'post', 'product') /* 'page', 'post', 'product' */
        
/* only include this line if a slug has been specified. e.g.
      and post_name = 'specifiedSlug'

from w0lap_abj404_redirects r

left outer join w0lap_posts p
on r.final_dest = p.id

left outer join w0lap_terms t
on r.final_dest = t.term_id

where   r.url in ('/blog/page/20/73f335e371f3b52d8c846e61fe3fdc3a10ef9c0426ba5a8e355075b3e342c067filenameÊtegory/uncategorized/', '/blog/page/20/73f335e371f3b52d8c846e61fe3fdc3a10ef9c0426ba5a8e355075b3e342c067filenameÊtegory/uncategorized')
        /* a disabled value of '1' means in the trash. */
        and r.disabled = 0 
        and r.status in (1, 2)
        and r.type not in (0)

        /* only include the redirect if the page exists or the destination is external. */
        and (p.id is not null or t.term_id is not null or r.type = 4)

-- make sure the first url appears first.
order by (CASE
			when r.url = '/blog/page/20/73f335e371f3b52d8c846e61fe3fdc3a10ef9c0426ba5a8e355075b3e342c067filenameÊtegory/uncategorized/' then 1

			else 'Unknown'
         end),
         r.timestamp desc

from w0lap_abj404_redirects r

on r.final_dest = p.id

select r.* 
from w0lap_abj404_redirects r

left outer join w0lap_posts p
on r.final_dest = p.id

left outer join w0lap_terms t
on r.final_dest = t.term_id

where   r.url in ('/blog/page/20/6fe23526427b0098bf5376ce415662ef8589cd4300ef68ab72487c303b757dd1filenameÊtegory/japan-tengsu/', '/blog/page/20/6fe23526427b0098bf5376ce415662ef8589cd4300ef68ab72487c303b757dd1filenameÊtegory/japan-tengsu')
        /* a disabled value of '1' means in the trash. */
        and r.disabled = 0 
        and r.status in (1, 2)
        and r.type not in (0)

        /* only include the redirect if the page exists or the destination is external. */
        and (p.id is not null or t.term_id is not null or r.type = 4)

-- make sure the first url appears first.
order by (CASE
			when r.url = '/blog/page/20/6fe23526427b0098bf5376ce415662ef8589cd4300ef68ab72487c303b757dd1filenameÊtegory/japan-tengsu/' then 1
			when r.url = '/blog/page/20/6fe23526427b0098bf5376ce415662ef8589cd4300ef68ab72487c303b757dd1filenameÊtegory/japan-tengsu' then 2
			else 'Unknown'
         end),
         r.timestamp desc

select r.* 
from w0lap_abj404_redirects r

left outer join w0lap_posts p
on r.final_dest = p.id

left outer join w0lap_terms t
on r.final_dest = t.term_id

where   r.url in ('/asistencia-humanitaria-que-es/8598792eafefc42d419ba09f2c05076e5aba738f8a6e6bd977f4ba121eb68115filenameÊrt/', '/asistencia-humanitaria-que-es/8598792eafefc42d419ba09f2c05076e5aba738f8a6e6bd977f4ba121eb68115filenameÊrt')
        /* a disabled value of '1' means in the trash. */
        and r.disabled = 0 
        and r.status in (1, 2)
        and r.type not in (0)

        /* only include the redirect if the page exists or the destination is external. */
        and (p.id is not null or t.term_id is not null or r.type = 4)

-- make sure the first url appears first.
order by (CASE
			when r.url = '/asistencia-humanitaria-que-es/8598792eafefc42d419ba09f2c05076e5aba738f8a6e6bd977f4ba121eb68115filenameÊrt/' then 1
			when r.url = '/asistencia-humanitaria-que-es/8598792eafefc42d419ba09f2c05076e5aba738f8a6e6bd977f4ba121eb68115filenameÊrt' then 2
			else 'Unknown'
         end),
         r.timestamp desc

       wp_posts.post_type,
       wp_posts.post_parent,
       wp_posts.post_title,

       /* the depth is only here to initialize the value to something. later it's used for sorting. */
       '0' as depth,

       usefulterms.grouped_terms,
       
       plc.url

from w0lap_posts wp_posts

left outer join (
        /* This selects posts that have the exclude keys set in woocommerce. 
            The exclude keys are all aggregated on one line with group_concat().   */
    	select wptr.object_id,
               group_concat(wpt.name) as grouped_terms
	from w0lap_term_relationships wptr
    
        left outer join w0lap_terms wpt
        on wptr.term_taxonomy_id = wpt.term_id
        and wpt.name in ('exclude-from-search', 'exclude-from-catalog')
    
	where wpt.name is not null

    	group by wptr.object_id

	) usefulterms
on wp_posts.ID = usefulterms.object_id

left outer join w0lap_abj404_permalink_cache plc
on wp_posts.ID = plc.id

from w0lap_abj404_redirects r

left outer join w0lap_posts p
on r.final_dest = p.id

left outer join w0lap_terms t
on r.final_dest = t.term_id

where   r.url in ('/blog/page/16/57324d5982c160f677e0c3d49dc897b3799b078ef232b1cca186280d72abe321filenameÊtegory/japan-tengsu/', '/blog/page/16/57324d5982c160f677e0c3d49dc897b3799b078ef232b1cca186280d72abe321filenameÊtegory/japan-tengsu')
        /* a disabled value of '1' means in the trash. */
        and r.disabled = 0 
        and r.status in (1, 2)
        and r.type not in (0)

        /* only include the redirect if the page exists or the destination is external. */
        and (p.id is not null or t.term_id is not null or r.type = 4)

-- make sure the first url appears first.
order by (CASE
			when r.url = '/blog/page/16/57324d5982c160f677e0c3d49dc897b3799b078ef232b1cca186280d72abe321filenameÊtegory/japan-tengsu/' then 1

			else 'Unknown'
         end),
         r.timestamp desc

on r.final_dest = p.id

select r.* 
from w0lap_abj404_redirects r

left outer join w0lap_posts p
on r.final_dest = p.id

left outer join w0lap_terms t
on r.final_dest = t.term_id

where   r.url in ('/blog/page/16/2224fe69251643d70cb125afa830db0f35ee3a4bbb4f137a39752faf23854285filenameÊtegory/æ—¥æœ¬è—¤ç´ pchome/', '/blog/page/16/2224fe69251643d70cb125afa830db0f35ee3a4bbb4f137a39752faf23854285filenameÊtegory/æ—¥æœ¬è—¤ç´ pchome')
        /* a disabled value of '1' means in the trash. */
        and r.disabled = 0 
        and r.status in (1, 2)
        and r.type not in (0)

        /* only include the redirect if the page exists or the destination is external. */
        and (p.id is not null or t.term_id is not null or r.type = 4)

-- make sure the first url appears first.
order by (CASE
			when r.url = '/blog/page/16/2224fe69251643d70cb125afa830db0f35ee3a4bbb4f137a39752faf23854285filenameÊtegory/æ—¥æœ¬è—¤ç´ pchome/' then 1
			when r.url = '/blog/page/16/2224fe69251643d70cb125afa830db0f35ee3a4bbb4f137a39752faf23854285filenameÊtegory/æ—¥æœ¬è—¤ç´ pchome' then 2
			else 'Unknown'
         end),
         r.timestamp desc

select r.* 
from w0lap_abj404_redirects r

left outer join w0lap_posts p
on r.final_dest = p.id

left outer join w0lap_terms t
on r.final_dest = t.term_id

where   r.url in ('/ðŸ­', '/ðŸ­/')
        /* a disabled value of '1' means in the trash. */
        and r.disabled = 0 
        and r.status in (1, 2)
        and r.type not in (0)

        /* only include the redirect if the page exists or the destination is external. */
        and (p.id is not null or t.term_id is not null or r.type = 4)

-- make sure the first url appears first.
order by (CASE
			when r.url = '/ðŸ­' then 1
			when r.url = '/ðŸ­/' then 2
			else 'Unknown'
         end),
         r.timestamp desc

/* ------------------ /home/187653.cloudwaysapps.com/rykqssvdwt/public_html/wp-content/plugins/404-solution/includes/sql/getPublishedPagesAndPostsIDs.sql BEGIN ----- */ 

select wp_posts.id,
       wp_posts.post_type,
       wp_posts.post_parent,
       wp_posts.post_title,

       /* the depth is only here to initialize the value to something. later it's used for sorting. */
       '0' as depth,

       usefulterms.grouped_terms,
       
       plc.url

from w0lap_posts wp_posts

left outer join (
        /* This selects posts that have the exclude keys set in woocommerce. 
            The exclude keys are all aggregated on one line with group_concat().   */
    	select wptr.object_id,
               group_concat(wpt.name) as grouped_terms
	from w0lap_term_relationships wptr
    
        left outer join w0lap_terms wpt
        on wptr.term_taxonomy_id = wpt.term_id
        and wpt.name in ('exclude-from-search', 'exclude-from-catalog')
    
	where wpt.name is not null

    	group by wptr.object_id

	) usefulterms
on wp_posts.ID = usefulterms.object_id

left outer join w0lap_abj404_permalink_cache plc
on wp_posts.ID = plc.id

where wp_posts.post_status = 'publish'
      and lcase(wp_posts.post_type) in ('page', 'post', 'product') /* 'page', 'post', 'product' */
        
/* only include this line if a slug has been specified. e.g.
      and post_name = 'specifiedSlug'
 */
 and wp_posts.post_name = 'ðŸ­' 
 
/*  */

/* only include this line if a search term has been specified. e.g.
      and lower(post_name) like 'searchTerm'

/*  */

/* only include this line if it's been specified. e.g.
      and abs(plc.url_length - 100) <= 6

select r.* 
from w0lap_abj404_redirects r

left outer join w0lap_posts p
on r.final_dest = p.id

left outer join w0lap_terms t
on r.final_dest = t.term_id

where   r.url in ('/ðŸ­', '/ðŸ­/')
        /* a disabled value of '1' means in the trash. */
        and r.disabled = 0 
        and r.status in (1, 2)
        and r.type not in (0)

        /* only include the redirect if the page exists or the destination is external. */
        and (p.id is not null or t.term_id is not null or r.type = 4)

-- make sure the first url appears first.

			when r.url = '/ðŸ­' then 1
			when r.url = '/ðŸ­/' then 2
			else 'Unknown'
         end),
         r.timestamp desc

/* ------------------ /home/187653.cloudwaysapps.com/rykqssvdwt/public_html/wp-content/plugins/404-solution/includes/sql/getPublishedPagesAndPostsIDs.sql BEGIN ----- */ 

select wp_posts.id,
       wp_posts.post_type,
       wp_posts.post_parent,
       wp_posts.post_title,

       /* the depth is only here to initialize the value to something. later it's used for sorting. */
       '0' as depth,

       usefulterms.grouped_terms,
       
       plc.url

from w0lap_posts wp_posts

left outer join (
        /* This selects posts that have the exclude keys set in woocommerce. 
            The exclude keys are all aggregated on one line with group_concat().   */
    	select wptr.object_id,
               group_concat(wpt.name) as grouped_terms
	from w0lap_term_relationships wptr
    
        left outer join w0lap_terms wpt
        on wptr.term_taxonomy_id = wpt.term_id
        and wpt.name in ('exclude-from-search', 'exclude-from-catalog')
    
	where wpt.name is not null

    	group by wptr.object_id

	) usefulterms
on wp_posts.ID = usefulterms.object_id

left outer join w0lap_abj404_permalink_cache plc
on wp_posts.ID = plc.id

where wp_posts.post_status = 'publish'
      and lcase(wp_posts.post_type) in ('page', 'post', 'product') /* 'page', 'post', 'product' */
        
/* only include this line if a slug has been specified. e.g.

/* ------------------ /home/187653.cloudwaysapps.com/rykqssvdwt/public_html/wp-content/plugins/404-solution/includes/sql/getPermalinkFromURL.sql BEGIN ----- */ 

select r.* 
from w0lap_abj404_redirects r

left outer join w0lap_posts p
on r.final_dest = p.id

left outer join w0lap_terms t
on r.final_dest = t.term_id

where   r.url in ('/ðŸ­', '/ðŸ­/')
        /* a disabled value of '1' means in the trash. */
        and r.disabled = 0 
        and r.status in (1, 2)
        and r.type not in (0)

        /* only include the redirect if the page exists or the destination is external. */
        and (p.id is not null or t.term_id is not null or r.type = 4)

-- make sure the first url appears first.
order by (CASE
			when r.url = '/ðŸ­' then 1
			when r.url = '/ðŸ­/' then 2
			else 'Unknown'
         end),
         r.timestamp desc

       wp_posts.post_type,
       wp_posts.post_parent,
       wp_posts.post_title,

       '0' as depth,

       usefulterms.grouped_terms,
       
       plc.url

from w0lap_posts wp_posts

left outer join (
        /* This selects posts that have the exclude keys set in woocommerce. 
            The exclude keys are all aggregated on one line with group_concat().   */
    	select wptr.object_id,
               group_concat(wpt.name) as grouped_terms
	from w0lap_term_relationships wptr
    
        left outer join w0lap_terms wpt
        on wptr.term_taxonomy_id = wpt.term_id
        and wpt.name in ('exclude-from-search', 'exclude-from-catalog')
    
	where wpt.name is not null

    	group by wptr.object_id

	) usefulterms
on wp_posts.ID = usefulterms.object_id

left outer join w0lap_abj404_permalink_cache plc
on wp_posts.ID = plc.id

/* ------------------ /home/187653.cloudwaysapps.com/rykqssvdwt/public_html/wp-content/plugins/404-solution/includes/sql/getPermalinkFromURL.sql BEGIN ----- */ 

select r.* 
from w0lap_abj404_redirects r

left outer join w0lap_posts p
on r.final_dest = p.id

left outer join w0lap_terms t
on r.final_dest = t.term_id

where   r.url in ('/À', '/À/')
        /* a disabled value of '1' means in the trash. */
        and r.disabled = 0 
        and r.status in (1, 2)
        and r.type not in (0)

        /* only include the redirect if the page exists or the destination is external. */
        and (p.id is not null or t.term_id is not null or r.type = 4)

-- make sure the first url appears first.
order by (CASE
			when r.url = '/À' then 1
			when r.url = '/À/' then 2
			else 'Unknown'
         end),
         r.timestamp desc

select wp_posts.id,
       wp_posts.post_type,
       wp_posts.post_parent,
       wp_posts.post_title,

       /* the depth is only here to initialize the value to something. later it's used for sorting. */
       '0' as depth,

       usefulterms.grouped_terms,
       
       plc.url

from w0lap_posts wp_posts

left outer join (
        /* This selects posts that have the exclude keys set in woocommerce. 
            The exclude keys are all aggregated on one line with group_concat().   */
    	select wptr.object_id,
               group_concat(wpt.name) as grouped_terms
	from w0lap_term_relationships wptr
    
        left outer join w0lap_terms wpt
        on wptr.term_taxonomy_id = wpt.term_id
        and wpt.name in ('exclude-from-search', 'exclude-from-catalog')
    
	where wpt.name is not null

    	group by wptr.object_id

	) usefulterms
on wp_posts.ID = usefulterms.object_id

left outer join w0lap_abj404_permalink_cache plc
on wp_posts.ID = plc.id

where wp_posts.post_status = 'publish'
      and lcase(wp_posts.post_type) in ('page', 'post', 'product') /* 'page', 'post', 'product' */
        
/* only include this line if a slug has been specified. e.g.
      and post_name = 'specifiedSlug'
 */
 and wp_posts.post_name = 'À'

/* only include this line if a search term has been specified. e.g.
      and lower(post_name) like 'searchTerm'

/*  */

/* only include this line if it's been specified. e.g.
      and abs(plc.url_length - 100) <= 6

/*  */

and ( usefulterms.grouped_terms is null or 
	  usefulterms.grouped_terms not like '%exclude-from-search%'
	  or usefulterms.grouped_terms not like '%exclude-from-catalog%'

/* ------------------ /home/187653.cloudwaysapps.com/rykqssvdwt/public_html/wp-content/plugins/404-solution/includes/sql/getPermalinkFromURL.sql BEGIN ----- */ 

select r.* 
from w0lap_abj404_redirects r

left outer join w0lap_posts p
on r.final_dest = p.id

left outer join w0lap_terms t
on r.final_dest = t.term_id

where   r.url in ('/ðŸ­', '/ðŸ­/')
        /* a disabled value of '1' means in the trash. */
        and r.disabled = 0 
        and r.status in (1, 2)
        and r.type not in (0)

        /* only include the redirect if the page exists or the destination is external. */
        and (p.id is not null or t.term_id is not null or r.type = 4)

-- make sure the first url appears first.
order by (CASE
			when r.url = '/ðŸ­' then 1
			when r.url = '/ðŸ­/' then 2
			else 'Unknown'
         end),
         r.timestamp desc

select wp_posts.id,
       wp_posts.post_type,
       wp_posts.post_parent,
       wp_posts.post_title,

       /* the depth is only here to initialize the value to something. later it's used for sorting. */
       '0' as depth,

       usefulterms.grouped_terms,
       
       plc.url

from w0lap_posts wp_posts

left outer join (
        /* This selects posts that have the exclude keys set in woocommerce. 
            The exclude keys are all aggregated on one line with group_concat().   */
    	select wptr.object_id,
               group_concat(wpt.name) as grouped_terms
	from w0lap_term_relationships wptr
    
        left outer join w0lap_terms wpt
        on wptr.term_taxonomy_id = wpt.term_id
        and wpt.name in ('exclude-from-search', 'exclude-from-catalog')
    
	where wpt.name is not null

    	group by wptr.object_id

	) usefulterms
on wp_posts.ID = usefulterms.object_id

left outer join w0lap_abj404_permalink_cache plc
on wp_posts.ID = plc.id

where wp_posts.post_status = 'publish'
      and lcase(wp_posts.post_type) in ('page', 'post', 'product') /* 'page', 'post', 'product' */
        
/* only include this line if a slug has been specified. e.g.
